<user>113403324192991608062<//user><Name>Erick Escamilla<//Name>< time>
1515343327056</time>
<rate>5<//rate>< review>
We've stayed at a lot of motel 6's. NONE  have  hair dryers, or irons, shampoo or lotions, or those kind of ammenedies, you need to be aware of that before you stay at any of them. That's how they are. It's rare they have microwaves in the room or fridges. This one had both. We always pack a dryer and know what were getting a motel 6, which is kind of nice because we are rarely surprised.

It's easy for us because we have a dog, (no extra fees or deposits for pets)  and don't normally spend a lot of time in our rooms. Point is, we just need a clean place to crash. This one in particular was exactly that. Person working the desk was nice. The room had a microwave and fridge (most we've stayed at do not). The TV was a good size and most of all, it's exactly what we expected.

For under $60 for the night, (weekend in January)  it's a great deal for 2 adults (were in our early 30s) and one big dog. We stayed here after a day trip of driving, seeing salvation mountain, east Jesus, Bombay Beach (weird stuff we've always wanted to check out). It was a good in between spot for us. After all day sight seeing, we had dinner across the street at the restaurant, skipped over to vons for a few items and drove about 15 min to go bowling in El Centro. All in all, good stay.</review>

<review>While it was great to have two power outlets, one of them on the east side of the room on the left-hand side of the bed in the most east corner of the room, did not want to work at all, even for the bed light it was supposed to illuminate above at least one of the beds.

Secondly, at first, our room keys did not want to work being inserted into our front door of our room. While I was relieved to hear that they worked for the back door, it would've been great to get our first impression of the room walking into the beautiful blue doors that resided in the courtyard of the property. The courtyard however on the other hand, was most definitely on-point.

Lastly, it would've been nice to have a TV that allowed for me to connect my laptop's display to it and allowed me to navigate the web using the LCD TV as a monitor, mainly because I accidentally cracked my Macbook's screen recently. Not your fault at all, just would've been cool to have been able to switch video inputs on the TV to my Macbook Pro.

Overall though, this is an outstanding value, especially for being this close to extraordinarily beautiful places, such as Coachella and the Salton Sea, and within a reasonable drive to the California coastline and Calexico/Mexicali. Breakfast was delicious, coffee was fresh, and customer service outstanding! Keep up the great work!< /review>< pics>

<time>1413824253723</time>< rating>

< text>
Alright, so for starters, let me talk a little bit about why I came here.

I recently moved to the area and actually had my computer shipped all the way from Wisconsin. Shipping my gaming desktop was quite a scary thing to do but I really had no other choice because I wasn't about to make a flight back from California to Wisconsin then back again for the computer. This option turned out to be cheaper.

When the computer made its way over here the external video card was actually not working (it had worked fine in the past), but on-board video actually got the job done. Didn't know why that was the case but I really didn't mind all too much. So about a week or two into using it, while I'm playing a game, the computer video just completely shuts off, everything - HDMI, DVI, VGA - nothing would work.

That's what brought me to Orange County Computer Repair.  I didn't really have the tools to fix the issue myself as I recently moved and I didn't exactly know what the issue was, so I decided to be a little lazy and let someone else take over. It could have been anything, from the power supply not working correctly, the motherboard being completely broken (this is actually a fairly new motherboard) or some other issue.

Anyway, I have this company fix the problem and they call me back fairly quickly and tell me I have two issues. 1., the obvious - the video card isn't working and they can order a new one of the same kind to be shipped to their place and 2., something really stupid with the processor's heat sink. I told them not to order another video card because the cost would be $200 more compared to $150 for just "repairing the processor's heat sink" (which I still regard to be a little overpriced). They said they would have it fixed the same day by 3:00pm - they had called me almost around noon.

So for probably less than three hours of work, they had my computer finished and I went to pick it up a few days later. I did not sign the "satisfied customer line" because I was a little skeptical of that and I didn't want to be trapped if the issue was not fixed. And alas, I go home, test it out, and it doesn't work. So I called them back and I was pretty pissed, but held my tongue, and they tell me that I actually need to take out the video card for my on-board video to even work. After that the computer booted up just fine, which led me to believe that they possibly jipped me of $130 more than they should have.

So for not telling me that I needed to take out my defective video card out for the computer to even function, I removed one star. For being extremely over-priced, I removed another. (Not fair prices at all, at least in my experience.)

Hopefully they did not steal $130 out of my wallet, but who knows? I should have taken the video card out in the first place. I'll have to pass on that bit of information to someone else in my life story who has that issue.

However, I do have two good things to say. 1 - They fixed the issue, or at least told me how to fix my issue for $130 and 2 - They were pretty decently fast. Next time I would probably have them inspect the issue and see what I can do myself.

Three stars.<//text>

<Text>In June, 2020 we filed a warranty claim with Milgard for replacing 15 of our windows (that were under the lifetime warranty). There was condensation between the double panes.
A few weeks later I was given a contact who would handle the claim. I followed all of the requirements to submit the details. By the way, the contact was not polite and condescending.
I found a different support person and she was professional.  She scheduled a date that the work would be done, Sept 10th, between 7-4. We were required to prepare the windows for the appt by taking down the screens and the window coverings. This took us time, tools, etc. We had to arrange for someone to be at the house on that (mid-week) day because it is our ski cabin.
At 8 am on Sept 10th, I got a call that no one would be coming since none of the replacement windows had been ordered yet. They said that the appt. was rescheduled to Nov. 17th. I was not happy and asked for a followup call from the manager. Nobody followed up.
A week before the 11/17 appt. we called Milgard to make sure that they had all the materials. At first they said that they were missing one piece, then they said all materials were ready.
We have taken down all of the window coverings and arranged for someone to be at the cabin for this midweek appt. Today, two days before the appt. Milgard called to cancel the appt. They would not give me a reschedule date.
Also, I am unable to talk with anyone in management to get any kind of answer. It's a nightmare. We have no leverage. They are doing everything to slow down the process. The management is terribly unprofessional in all departments. I have heard from receptionist a tip to call early or they won't answer the phones, another rep said the manager is not working today and there is no backup, and a supervisor said the manager was out because, well, you know, it's Friday.
The excuses are "family emergency", "COVID", unprecedented times, this is just happening to you, a series of unfortunate events. I would say to anyone who is buying these windows because of the advertised warranty, Don't buy it. <rating>3< /rating><review>Our new windows were delivered with bowed casings and did not work as expected. There was no immediate technical support available or offered to us. < review>
UNPROFESSIONAL. I ordered Milgard replacement windows through Lowes. About a month later I got a call from Milgard wanting to deliver my order the next day between 11-12. Well, not very convenient since I work during the day, and only one day notice, but I say I can make it work since I wasn't given a choice. I take vacation time and wait. No one shows up. At 12 I call the Milgard dispatch. They call the driver to find out where he is. I'm on hold over 5 minutes. Dispatch comes back, says driver is driving so they didn't answer the phone (why did it take 5 minutes if didn't talk to anyone?). Fine. I go back to work. I get a call at 1 from a delivery guy wanting to schedule since I missed the delivery. Now, the guy on the phone had to relay everything I said to someone else, so there were at least 2 people in the truck.  So the whole "driver didn't answer because they were driving" sounds like a lie to me. Is the guy that drives the only one allowed to answer the phone? I was quick to point out that I didn't miss the delivery, I was there from 11-12. After conferring with the guy #2, guy #1 insisted they were there between 11-12. That is obviously a lie, because; A) I was there at the time they told me to be there, and B) I went back and looked at the security camera footage. They were there at 9:26am. So, Milgard delivery personal lied, and I suspect the dispatcher did as well. I have spent thousands on replacement windows, but apparently that's not enough to be treated with respect by Milgard. Stuff happens, I get it, but don't lie to your customer.< /review>

< review>
The lifetime guarantee of window replacements for original homeowner is fantastic.  I have about twenty or twenty five Milgard windows, and 4 of them got leaky with condensation between panes. It took a while to reserve the estimator's visit and then get the technicians in there, but when they came, they did a good job and even replaced some old weatherstripping without that being part of the job order.  My only real complaint is that the guys tracked mud and dirt into the house (we have two door mats, one inside and one outside and they didn't seem to use these.  They did not come equipped with "contractor shoe covers" either.
